<Time>1611015031123<//Time><username>Vicky Leung< /username>< Text>
Good milk tea spot with bobas sweetened with brown sugar (not honey boba finally). I don't know when the trend of honey boba started but it ruins the tea flavor in my opinion. We got their dark roasted oolong milk tea and hojicha milk tea (less ice and less sweet).
If you like less sweet milk tea, you can even go with unsweeten since the boba has a nice brown sugar sweetness to it (which is what I'll do next time). Their hojicha milk tea uses ground tea powder (similar to matcha) which brings a slight grainy texture than regular milk tea. It packs a big punch of tea flavor. Their dark roasted oolong is very smooth and balanced. you can also pick alternate milk choices. You can order from their website for pick up or delivery.</Text>

I visit the Jiaren Cafe weekly. Jiaren (meaning "elegant lady"in the Chinese language) aptly describes my experience of its proprietress, Jaden, and (even with the constrictions of COVID) the ambiance of her establishment. <Response>{'time': 1573667483695, 'text': 'Hi Fidel, we are still in soft opening and trying to figure out the best ingredients for our products. We use high quality coffee beans from Ritual Coffee and ceremonial grade of Matcha. We make our own chai from scratch because we do not want to serve the powder form of chai product in market. After serious research we decided on investing in Synesso MVP espresso machine to make the best espresso according to the taste profile that we want to achieve. We understand everyone has different preference for the taste of coffee. It is unfortunate that what we think is great does not fit into what you are looking for. The price we have shows the qualities that we want to provide for our customers. The unsweetened almond milk is only an option that we provide besides regular almond milk.\n\nThank you for your feedbacks, and allowing us the opportunity to respond to your review to show our passion for our coffee, matcha and other drinks. And you are always welcome to stop by!'}</Response><Text>Been here a few times, the coffee is ok. It honestly tastes like something I could make at home. I genuinely got the feeling that they went out and got an espresso machine just to open this coffee shop, without researching   how to make a really good cup of coffee or espresso.

I got a chai latte with almond milk and a regular latte with regular milk.  Both were fine, one thing I noticed is that they use Kirkland brand almond milk, which is fine if the latte were $3, but not for $6 - there are better almond milks out there that should be used if that's how much the latte costs. The regular latte was $5, I wouldn't mind paying this for my coffee either if it was really good, but currently I think there is a lot of  room for improvement.

With that being said, the place is super nice, they have cool items for sale such as tea sets and other neat items. My dad was coming out for a 2 week visit and it wasn't until the last minute we realized we needed to find a wheelchair for him, to rent (and he was arriving the next day). I starting searching for rentals and I came across cloud of goods. The website was simple. I thought well let me look for another site just as a backup in case because it was already later in the day and I was not certain I would hear back. Within minutes I received a text message from Stacy from cloud letting me know that she received my message and so I texted her details and then called her to arrange it. They have a delivery time but for a small additional fee they will deliver the wheelchair based on your schedule. They were there exactly when they said they would be and delivered the chair. It was lightweight and perfect for the time my dad was here. <date>1555519522484< /date><response>None<//response><Name>Valerie Tillman< /Name><Rate>5</Rate>< text>
On 2/22/17, Wednesday, I drove to the AT&T store after taking care of an unforseen emergency. The phone I originally had froze and AT&T shipped a new one.
Once I entered two employees were standing with their tablets greeting people. This particular employee 'Marlion Barnett' immediately stated, " Welcome to AT&T How Can I Help You Today"? He smiled and walked over to me.
This was extremely professional and build an awesome repor during my visit. Most places you walk in employees become great pretenders like their too busy and avoid helping customer's.
"NOT MARLION!"
I explained the situation and he offered me a seat asked various questions in order to troubleshoot and fix the problem.
Marlion was a 'Superb' listener and after I explained, his communication and walking me through the various steps for the transferring of information from the defective to new cellphone was of "Expertise" and importance.
This employee was so "Outstanding" I asked him to please go get the store manager and he really didn't have any idea as to why nor did he question, merely, respecting my request.
